1 Introduction  
The CFTC operates a comprehensive system of collecting information on market participants as part of 
its market surveillance program. Under regulations set out in Part 16, promulgated under the 
Commodity Exchange Act (CEA), the Commission collects market data and position information from 
exchanges.  
To ensure privacy of the information provided , the CFTC has assigned confidential reporting numbers to 
reporting firms and traders. The Commission is prohibited under  Section s 8 of the CEA and 7 USC 12  
from publicly disclosing any person’s positions, transactions, or trade secrets, except under limited 
circumstances.  
This guidebook for Part 16 – Clearing Member Reports is bein g issued to accommodate the additional 
data requirement to report commodity contract trading volumes attributable to block trades1, 
promulgated in response to the Part 38  – Designated Contract Markets  rule update s regarding the 
prevention of market disrupt ion, the preservation of trade data,  and the ability to accurately reconstruct 
trading activities2. 
2 Technical Requirements  
Please forward questions regarding format, content, and transmission of Part 16 data submissions to the 
CFTC at (TBD) Part16TechSupport@cftc.gov  . 
2.1 Formats  
2.1.1  File Format for Part 16 Reporting  
Compliant XML formats for reporting include the FIXML Position Report and Market Data Full Report , 
which is  described in the FIX Protocol Global Technical Committee and Futures Industry Association, 
CFTC Large Trader Reporting for Commodities Swaps, Revision 1.5, January 14, 2012 .  (See 
http://www. fixprotocol.org/specifications/EP140  for more details .) 
2.1.2  Map Part 16 Data  to FIXML  
See the data dictionary tables for mapping gu idance . 
                                                            
1 §16.01(a)(2)(vi)  
2 §38.251(c), §38.251(d), §38.254(a), §38.254(b), §38.450, and §38.950.  
Commodity Futures Trading Commission  
Office of Data and Technology  Guidebook for Part 16

2.2 Part 16 Submission Procedure  
Follow the step s below to submit  a Part 16 Report:  
1. Create the report(s) and consolidate the report(s) into an XML -formatted file following the 
FIXML Position Report or FIXML Market Data  Full Report . 
2. Name the file(s) using the Part 16 Reporting file name format.  
3. Assemble and compress the files.  
4. Connect to the CFTC FTP site . 
5. Transmit t he electronic ally formatted records to the Commission using Secure FTP.  
2.2.1  Reporting Schedules  
Section 16.01(d)(2) directs the exchanges to submit § 16.01 early market data ( delta factor and 
settlement price) reports no later than 7:00 AM on the next business day followi ng a reporting day. 
Similarly, Section 16.01(d)(2) directs reporting entities to submit § 16.00 clearing member position 
reports and § 16.01 permanent market data reports no later than 12:00 on the business day 
following the reporting day. Unless otherwise  specified by the Commission or its designee, the 
stated time is U.S. Eastern Time for information concerning markets located in that time zone, and 
U.S. Central T ime for information concerning markets located in that time zone.  
Reporting Time for § 16.00 and § 16.01 Reports  
7:00 AM (Local Mkt Time)  EMKTDATA  
12:00 PM (Local Mkt Time)  PMKTDATA , CMPOS  
The definition of business day in § 1.3 of the Commission’s regulations includes all days except 
Sundays and holidays. For the purposes of complying with Part 16, reporting entities may elect to 
not consider Saturdays to be a business day, as Saturday is n ot commonly known as such. Instead, 
clearing organizations and reporting entities may submit Part 16 data records under the schedule 
displayed in the following table. In the table, the submission day is the day of the week that the 
relevant report for the associated reporting day is expected by the Commission. The time during the 
day that reports are expected is unchanged from § 16.01(d)(2).  
The reporting schedule displayed in the table below does not take into account any holidays. To the 
extent that a U. S. Federal government holiday falls on either the submission day, it is permissible for 
the submission of the applicable Part 16 data record to occur on the business day immediately after 
the usual submission day. Please note that any submission made under  Part 16 can be made prior to 
the relevant submission day shown below. Early submission is beneficial in that it may allow the 
Commission to review your submission earlier and provide more timely feedback regarding the 
acceptability of the file structure a nd data contents.  
Commodity Futures Trading Commission  
Office of Data and Technology  Guidebook for Part 16

2.2.2  Format the  Data for Transmission  
Segr egate t he records by report type and consolida te them  into an XML -formatted file following the 
FIXML Position Report  or FIXML Market Data  Full Report , as described in section 3.1, Data Dictionary 
for Clearing Member Reports (pg. 10) or section 4.5, Data Dictionary for Market Data Reports (pg. 
26).  
Some characters have a special meaning in XML. If you place a character like "<" inside an XML 
element, it will generate an error because the parser interprets it as the start of a new element. This 
will generate an XML error:  
<message>if salary  < 1000 then</message>  
To avoid this error, replace the "<" character with an entity reference : 
<message>if salary &lt; 1000 then</message>  
There are 5 predefined entity references in XML:  
&lt; < less than  
&gt;  > greater than  
&amp;  & ampersand  
&apos;  ' apostrophe  
&quot;  " quotation mark  
If the indicated characters appear in data fields , ensure they are replaced  with the appropriate 
entity reference value.  
2.2.3  Name the File(s)  
File Naming Convention  - Position Report  
The file name for submission should be created in the following manner:  
CMPOS_[ORGTYP]_[IDENT] _[YYYYMMDD].fixml  (Clearing Mbr Position Rpt)  
File Naming Convention  - Market Data Report(s)  
The file name for submission should be created in the following manner:  
                                                            
3 Interpreted as the next open trading date, usually the Monday following Friday or the next date after an 
intervening holiday.

EMKTDATA_[ORGTYP]_[IDENT]_[YYYYMMDD].fixml  (Early Mkt Data Rpt)  
PMKTDATA_[ORGTYP]_[IDENT]_[YYYYMMDD].fixml  (Permanent Mkt Data Rpt)  
File Naming Convention - Test Files  
Data providers can test their submissions by appending the string “TEST” to the end of their file 
names.   
CMPOS_[ORGTYP]_[IDENT]_[YYYYMMDD]_TEST.fixml  (Clearing Mbr Position Rpt)  
EMKTDATA_[ORGTYP]_[IDENT]_[YYYYMMDD]_TEST.fixml  (Early Mkt Data Rpt)  
PMKTDATA_[ORGTYP]_[IDENT]_[YYYYMMDD]_TEST.fixml  (Permanent Mkt Data Rpt)  
File Naming Convention – On Behalf Files  
Third parties  can submit reports on behalf of a contract market . Indicate that the file is submitted on 
behalf of the responsible contract ma rket by appending the  submitter  identifying code to the end of 
the file names. The f ollowing file names represent files submitted by OCC on behalf of  a contract 
market . 
CMPOS_[ORGTYP]_[IDENT]_[YYYYMMDD]_XOCC.fixml  (Clearing Mbr Position Rpt)  
EMKTDATA_[ORG TYP]_[IDENT]_[YYYYMMDD]_XOCC.fixml  (Early Mkt Data Rpt)  
PMKTDATA_[ORGTYP]_[IDENT]_[YYYYMMDD]_XOCC.fixml  (Permanent Mkt Data Rpt)  
Your firm can contact our Technical Support representative at Part16TechSupport@cftc.gov  to verify  
the results of test data you have submitted.  
File Naming Convention – 80-Byte Files  
CFTC has a 2nd UAT environment set up to receive 80 -byte -test files.   Use the following naming 
convention for for 80 -byte test files:   
CMPOS_EX_[IDENT]_[YYYYMMDD]_TEST.test80dat  (Clearing Mbr Position Rpt)  
EMKTDATA_[IDENT]_[YYYYMMDD]_TEST.test80dat  (Early Mkt Data Rpt)  
PMKTDATA _[IDENT]_[YYYYMMDD]_TEST. test80dat  (Permanent Mkt Data Rpt)  
Third parties can submit reports on behalf of a contract market. Indicate that the file is submitted on 
behalf of the responsible contract market by appending the submitter identifying code to the end of 
the file names. The following file names represent files submitted by OCC on behalf of a contract 
market.  
CMPOS_IDENT]_[YYYYMMDD]_XOCC.TEST. test80dat  (Clearing Mbr Position Rpt)

FIXML reporting using the MktDataFull  fixml  
2.2.4  Assemble and Compress  the File(s)  
After  you as semble the data file, compress it  using the GZIP utility. The GZIP utility is freely available 
at http://www.gzip.org . Form t he GZIP file name by appending “.gz” to the compressed file’s name. 
Alternatively you may use WINZIP to compress and append “.zip” to the file name. The only 
acceptable archive file typs are .ZIP or .GZ . 
2.2.5  Connect to CFTC with Secure  FTP  
Connect to the CFTC  FTP site at traders.cftc.gov , and log  in us ing your account and password.  
The compressed files will be submitted to the CFTC via Secured File Transfer Protocol (SFTP).  Many 
entities providing Part 16 reporting alre ady have FTP or SFTP accounts. Reporting entities with SFTP 
accounts can continue to use those accounts for Part 16 reporting.  New reporters who do not 
already have an SFTP account, or reporters who only use non -secure FTP accounts, must re quest a 
Secure FTP account from the CFTC.  See Appendix A: SFTP Account Registation.  
Commodity Futures Trading Commission  
Office of Data and Technology  Guidebook for Part 16  
 
January 02, 2014   Page 6 of 560 
 
2.2.6  Transmit the File(s)  
Transfer the compressed file (s) using normal FTP commands.  
Upon receipt  of the file , software at the CFTC will ingest the file through our firewall an d begin 
processing the data.  
2.2.7  Data Validation and Error Handling  
Reports submitted to CFTC under Part 16 are subjected to several quality checks before final 
processing and promotion into the appropriate production database tables. All messages must first 
pass validation against the applicable reference XML standards (e.g., FIXML, FpML, CFTC Forms) for 
well-formedness and enumerated valid value sets. Messages passing initial XML validation are 
loaded into staging tables and individual records are further che cked against validation rules and 
valid value sets not enumerated in the XML schema. Records that pass the validation rules are 
promoted to the production database. Those that fail the validation rules are moved to error 
processing tables and grouped by ex ternal errors or internal errors for notification. External errors 
result in eMail notification to the reporting entity, identifying the specific record that failed 
validation and the reason(s) for the failure. Internal errors result in eMail notifications  to the 
appropriate CFTC organization for resolution and handling guidance.  
2.2.8  Error and Ommission Correction Handling  
Reporting markets shall file corrections to errors or omissions in data previously filed with the 
Commission pursuant to §16.00 and §16.01 using same format , coding structure , and electronic 
data submission procedures previously described in this section . To correct error s or omission s a 
firm must resubmit both corrected  report s for the affected day. The pair are reprocessed and 
replace existing data records for that day.  
Commodity Futures Trading Commission  
Office of Data and Technology  Guidebook for Part 16  
 
January 02, 2014   Page 7 of 560 
 
3 Information to Be Provided Under 
§16.00 Clearing Member Reports  
Under 17 CFR Part 16, reporting markets  must provide the Commission with confidential informat ion on 
the aggregate positions and trading activity for each of their clearing members. Each day, exchanges 
report each clearing member’s open long and short positions, purchases and sales, exchanges of futures 
for commodities or for derivatives , and futur es delivery notices for the previous trading day. This data is 
reported separately for proprietary and cus tomer accounts by futures month  and for options by puts 
and calls, expiration date , and strike price.  
Each reporting market shall submit to the Commis sion a report for each business day, showing for each 
clearing member, by proprietary and customer account, the following information separately for futures 
by commodity and by future, and, for options, by underlying futures contract for options on futures  
contracts or by underlying physical for options on physicals, and by put, by call, by expiration date and 
by strike price  (generally  reported  in terms of U.S. Dollars (USD) ): 
(1) The total of all long open contracts and the total of all short open contracts c arried at the end of 
the day covered by the report, excluding from open futures contracts the number of contracts 
against which delivery notices have been stopped or against which delivery notices have been 
issued by the clearing organization of the report ing market;  
(2) The quantity of contracts bought and the quantity of contracts sold during the day covered by 
the report;  
(3) The quantity of purchases of futures for commodities or for derivatives positions and the 
quantity of sales of futures for commodities or for derivatives positions which are included in 
the total quantity of contracts bought and sold during the day covered by the report, and the 
names of the clearing members who made the purchases or sales;  
(4) For futures, the quantity of the commodity fo r which delivery notices have been issued by the 
clearing organization of the reporting market and the quantity for which notices have been 
stopped during the day covered by the report.
Commodity Futures Trading Commission  
Office of Data and Technology  Guidebook for Part 16  
 
January 02, 2014    Page 8 of 560

  <Hdr MsgTyp ="AP" SID="[See Appendix A for valid exchange code values ]" TID="CFTC " Snt="2012 -09-14T09:30:47 -06:00 "/> 
  <!-- Position  Information  
    @RptID = [Report Identifier]  
    @BizDt = [Report Date] (format is YYYY -MM-DD)

    @Clrd = [Cleared Indicator] (0=Unc leared, 1=Cleared)

    @Ccy=[Currency] (Code for prevailing currency)

   </Pty>

       H = Clearing House / Clearing Organization, I = ISDA/FpML Prod XML, J = Option Price Reporting Authority,  
       K = ISDA/FpML Prod URL, L = Let ter of Credit, M = Marketplace -assigned Identifier)  
     @SecTyp = [CMDTYSWAP |  FUT |  OOC | OOF  | OPT ] ( CMDTYSWAP = Commodity Swap, FUT = Futures, OOC = Options on Combos, OOF = Options on 
Futures, OPT = Options)  
     @MMY = [ Delivery Year/Month ] Futures  only. (formats YYYYMM for month, YYYYMMDD for day, YYYYMMwN for week. A specific date  
       or can be appended to the MaturityMonthYear. For instance, if multiple standard products exist that mature in the same  
       Year and Month, but actually mature  at a different time, a value can be appended, such as "w" or "w2" to indicate week  
       as opposed to week 2 expiration. Likewise, the date (0 -3) can be appended to indicate a specific expiration (maturity  
       date).  
     @MatDt = [ Option Expirat ion Date] (format is YYYY -MM-DD; only used for Options)  
     @Mat Tm = [Option Expirat ion Time] (format is hh:mm:ss .sss[+|-]hh:mm ; only used for Options)  
     @StrkPx = [Strike Price] (for options only, format decimal number, e.g., 0.0000000000 ; only used f or Options ) 
     @OptPayoutTyp = [Opt Pay Indicator] (1=Vanilla, 2=Capped, 3=Binary)  
     @OptPayAmt = [Opt Pay Amount] (Option Pay Amount, required for @OptPayoutTyp=3)  
     @CapPx= [Cap Price] (for options only, format decimal number, e.g., 0.0000000000 ; only used for Options ) 
     @FlrPx = [Floor Price] (for options only, format decimal number, e.g., 0.00 ; only used for Options ) 
     @PutCall = [Put or Call Indicator] (0 = Put, 1 = Call ; only used for Options ) 
     @Exch = [ Use MIC code. See Appendix A for valid exchange code values. ) 
     @Desc = [Security Description ] The verbal description of the security -->

3.4 Validation Rules for Clearing Member Position Report (CMPOS)  
 Use 
FUT|OPT  Rule Description  Error Message  Error Type : Processing Status  
1. 1 F O Is Member Name provided by the 
reporter?  For Clearing Member Report  - Required Member 
Name is missing.  External: Bad Record is not processed i.e. not moved 
to ISS database but is moved to Errored table for 
external notification and Data Managers view.  
2. 2 F O Exchange Member Name does not 
match with that in CFTC System.  For Clearing Member Report  -  Invalid Exchange 
Member Name found  Internal (Record Not Processed):  Bad Record is not 
processed ,  i.e. not moved to ISS database. Once the 
data has been fixed in the CFTC System, the Data 
Manager will trigger the processing of these records 
from Errored table and push it to ISS Database.  
3.  F O Is Member ID provided by the reporter?  For Clearing Member Report  - Required Member ID 
is missing.  External: Bad Record is not processed i.e. not moved 
to ISS database but is moved to Errored table for 
external notification and Data Managers view.  
4.  F O Exchange Member ID not found  For Clearing Member Report  -  Invalid Exchange 
Member ID found  Internal (Record  Not Processed):  Bad Record is not 
processed   i.e. not moved to ISS database. Once the 
data has been fixed in the CFTC System, the Data 
Manager will trigger the processing of these records 
from Errored table and push it to ISS Database.  
5.  F O Long should be numeric  For Clearing Member Report  -  Long should be 
numeric.  External: The file will be rejected and the external user 
will be notified of the error with FIXML element and 
line number.  
6.  F O Short should be numeric  For Clearing Member Report  -  Short should be 
numeric.  External: The file will be rejected and the external user 
will be notified of the error with FIXML element and 
Commodity Futures Trading Commission  
Office of Data and Technology  Guidebook for Part 16  
 
January 02, 2014   Page 23 of 560 
 
 Use 
FUT|OPT  Rule Description  Error Message  Error Type : Processing Status  
line number.  
7.  F O Contracts Bought should be numeric  For Clearing Member Report  -  Contracts Bought 
should be numeric.  External: The file will be rejected and the external user 
will be notified of the error with FIXML element and 
line number.  
8.  F O Contracts Sold should be numeric  For Clearing Member Report  -  Contracts Sold 
should be numeric.  External: The file will be rejected and the external user 
will be notified of the error with FIXML element and 
line number.  
9.  F O EFPs Bought should be numeric  For Clearing Member Report  -  EFPs Bought should 
be numeric.  External: The file will be rejected and the external user 
will be notified of the error with FIXML element and 
line number.  
10.  F O EFPs Sold should be numeric  For Clearing Member Report  -  EFPs Sold should be 
numeric.  External: The file will be rejected and the external user 
will be notified of the error with FIXML element and 
line number.  
11.  F O EFSs Bought should be numeric8 For Clearing Member Report  -  EFSs Bought should 
be numeric.  External: The file will be rejected and the external user 
will be notified of the error with FIXML element and 
line number.  
12.  F O EFSs Sold should be numeric7 For Clearing Member Report  -  EFSs Sold should be 
numeric.  External: The file will be rejected and the external user 
will be notified of the error with FIXML element and 
line number.  
13.  F O Proprietary Or Customer Indicator must 
have one of the following values:  
 
Code        Description  For Clearing Member Report  -  The Proprietary Or 
Customer Indicator should be either House or 
Customer.  External: The file will be rejected and the external user 
will be notified of the error with FIXML element and 
line number.

H                House

the following values:  
 
Code         Description  
0            Put  
1           Call  For Clearing Member Report  -  The Put or Call 
Indicator should be either Put or Call.  External: The file will be rejected and the ext ernal user 
will be notified of the error with FIXML element and 
line number.  
15.  F O Is Exchange provided by the Reporter.  For Clearing Member Report  - Required Exchange 
Fields are missing.  External: Bad Record is not processed i.e. not moved 
to ISS database but is moved to Errored table for 
external notification and Data Managers view.  
16.  F O Is Valid Exchange provided  For Clearing Member Report  - Either Invalid 
Exchange code or Exchange Code has not   been set 
up in CFTC System  Internal (Record Not Processed):  Bad Record is not 
processed,  i.e. not moved to ISS database. Once the 
data has been fixed in the CFTC System, the Data 
Manager will trigger the processing of these records 
from Errored table and push it to ISS Database.  
17.  F O Is commodity provided by the Reporter.  For Clearing Member Report  - Required Commodity 
Fields are missing.  External: Bad Record is not processed i.e. not moved 
to ISS database but is moved to Errored table for 
external notification and Data Managers view.  
18.  F O Is Valid Commodity provided  For Clearing Member Report  - Either Invalid 
Commodity code or Commodity Code has not  been 
set up in CFTC System  Internal (Record Not Processed):  Bad Record is not 
processed  i.e. not moved to ISS database. Once the 
data has been fixed in the CFTC System, the Data 
Manager will trigger the processing of these records 
from Errored table and push it to ISS Database.  
19.  F O Is contract market active  For Clearing Member Report  - Contract market 
should be active.  Internal (Record Not Processed):  Bad Record is not 
processed,  i.e. not moved to ISS database. Once the 
data has been fixed in the CFTC System, the Data 
Manager will trigger the processing of these records

 Use

from Errored table and push it to ISS Database.  
20.  F  Is the futures expiration date a valid 
month for the contract  For Clearing Member Report  - Expiration Date does 
not contain valid Month for the contract.  Internal (Record Not Processed):  Bad Record is not 
processed ,  i.e. not moved to ISS database. Once the 
data has been fixed in the CFTC System, the Data 
Manager will trigger the processing of these records 
from Errored table and push it to ISS Database.  
21.  F O Is report date > last processing date  For Clearing Membe r Report  - Report Date should 
not be greater than the Last Processing Date.  Internal (Record Processed):  These are for 
informational purposes only. The record will be 
processed i.e. record will be moved to ISS database 
and internal users will be notified about it.  
22.  F O Report Date does not have valid Date 
Format (YYYY -MM -DD) For Clearing Member Report  -  Report Date must be 
in YYYY -MM -DD format.  External: The file will be rejected and the external user 
will be notified of the error with FIXML element and 
line number.  
23.   O Invalid Date Format for Expiration Date  For Clearing Member Report  - Invalid Expiration 
date Format.  External: The file will be rejected and the external user 
will be notified of the error with FIXML element and 
line number.  
24.   O If an indefinite date option, is the month 
valid  For Clearing Member Report  -  Invalid month found 
for Indefinite Date Option.  Internal  (Record Not Processed):  Bad Record is not 
processed ,  i.e. not moved to ISS database. Once the 
data has been fixed in the CFTC System, the Data 
Manager will trigger the processing of these records 
from Errored table and push it to ISS Database.  
25.  F O CROSS -FILE: For every CMPOS record 
there should be corresponding 
PMKTDATA record.  CMPOS: Referenced contract information missing 
from the Market Data Report, [insert contract 
information from the CMPOS].  
PMKTDATA: Data not provided for referenced 
contract in at least one CMPOS report, [insert External: 1) Bad Record is not processed i.e. not 
moved to ISS database but is moved to Errored table 
for external notification and Data Managers view. 2) 
Report error for e ach CMPOS that does not match a 
contract in the PMKTDATA. 3) Report error for missing 
PMKTDATA to match errored CMPOS.

contract information from the failed CMPOS].

option  only contract , all the underlying 
fields i.e. UnderlyingSecurity, 
UnderlyingSecurityType, 
UnderlyingSecurityExchange, 
UnderlyingSecurityDeliveryYearMonth

records.  
The value of following fields should be 
distinct in every record.  
 
 ReportDate  
 Exchange  
 Commodity  
 Unique Commodity Code  
 DeliveryYearMonth  
 StrikePrice  
 PutOrCall  
 MemberID  
 ProprietaryOrCustomer  
 ExpirationDate  
 For Clearing Member Report  -  Report contains 
duplicate records.  External: Bad Record is not processed i.e. not moved 
to ISS database but is moved to Errored table for 
external notification and Data Managers view.

1) For Op tions should be numeric.

be numeric  for this option and security type . External:  Bad Record is not processed i.e. not moved 
to ISS database but is moved to Errored table for 
external notification and Data Managers view.

4 Information to Be Provided Under 
§16.0 1 Market Data  Report s 
Each reporting market shall record for each business day the following information  
4.1 Trading Volume and Open Contracts  
Each reporting market shall report separately for futures by commodity and by future, and, for options, 
by underlying futures contract for options on futures contracts or by underlying physical for options on 
physicals, and by put, by call, b y expiration date and by strike price:  
(1) The option delta, where a delta system is used;  
(2) The total gross open contracts, excluding from futures those contracts against which notices 
have been stopped;  
(3) For futures, open contracts against which del ivery notices have been stopped on that business 
day;  
(4) The total volume of trading, excluding transfer trades or office trades;  
(5) The total volume of futures exchanged for commodities or for derivatives positions which are 
included in the total volume  of trading;  
(6) The total volume of block trades which are included in the total volume of trading9. 
4.2 Prices  
Each reporting market shall report  the following information separately for futures, by commodity and 
by future, and, for options, by underlying fu tures contract for options on futures contracts or by 
underlying physical for options on physicals, and by put, by call, by expiration date and by strike price:  
(1) For the trading session and for the opening and closing periods of trading as determined by  
each reporting market:  
(i) The lowest price of a sale or offer, whichever is lower, and the highest price of a sale or bid, 
whichever is higher, that the reporting market reasonably determines accurately reflect market 
conditions. If vacated or withdrawn,  bids and offers shall not be used in making this 
                                                            
9 Block Trading Volume is a new data requirement under Part 16, being driven by rule changes under Part 38.  
Commodity Futures Trading Commission  
Office of Data and Technology  Guidebook for Part 16  
 
January 02, 2014   Page 29 of 560 
 
determination. A bid is vacated if followed by a higher bid or price and an offer is vacated if 
followed by a lower offer or price.  
(ii) If there are no transactions, bids, or offers during the opening or c losing periods, the 
reporting market may record as appropriate:  
(A) The first price (in lieu of opening price data) or the last price (in lieu of closing price 
data) occurring during the trading session, clearly indicating that such prices are the first 
and the last price; or  
(B) Nominal opening or nominal closing prices which the reporting market reasonably 
determines accurately reflect market conditions, clearly indicating that such prices are 
nominal.  
(2) The settlement price established by each reportin g market or its clearing organization.  
(3) Additional information. Each reporting market shall record the following information with 
respect to transactions in commodity futures and commodity options on that reporting market:  
(i) The method used by the reporting market in determining nominal prices and settlement 
prices; and  
(ii) If discretion is used by the reporting market in determining the opening and closing ranges 
or the settlement prices, an explanation that certain discretion may be employed by t he 
reporting market and a description of the manner in which that discretion may be employed.  
4.3 Critical dates  
Each reporting market shall report to the Commission for each futures contract the first notice date and 
the last trading date and for each option contract the expiration date in accordance with paragraph (d) 
of this section.  
4.4 Form,  Manner  and Time of Filing 
Unless  otherwise  approved  by the Commission  or its designee,  reporting  markets  shall  submit  to the 
Commission  the information  specified  in paragraphs  4.1 (1) through  4.1 (5), 4.2 and 4.3 of this document 
as follows:  
(1) Using  the format,  coding  structure  and electronic  data  transmission  procedures  approved  in writing  
by the Commission  or its designee;  provided  however  , the information  shall  be made  available  to the 
Commission  or its designee  in hard  copy  upon  request;  and 
(2) When  each  such  form  of the data  is first available  but not later  than  7:00  a.m.  on the business  day 
following  the day to which  the information  pertains  for the delta  factor  and settlement  price  and not 
Commodity Futures Trading Commission  
Office of Data and Technology  Guidebook for Part 16  
 
January 02, 2014   Page 30 of 560 
 
later  than  12:00  p.m.  for the remainder  of the information.  Unless  otherwise  specified  by the 
Commission  or its designee,  the stated  time  is eastern  time  for information  concerning  markets  located  
in that time  zone,  and central  time  for information  concerning  all other  markets.  
Commodity Futures Trading Commission  
Office of Data and Technology  Guidebook for Part 16

the offset hours and minutes.

ss.sss[+ | -]hh:mm]  
17.  Delta Factor  E P A calculation of the expected change in 
an option's price given a one -unit 
change in the price of the underlying 
commodity or asset. Call options have 
positive deltas and p ut options have 
negative deltas. For example, the price 
of a call option with a delta of 0.5 
would be expected to increase by $0.50 
when the underlying commodity or 
asset’s price increases by $1.00.   The 
price of an put option with a delta of -
0.50 would b e expected to decrease by 
$0.50 when the underlying commodity 0.0000000000  - 1.0000000000  FIXML/Batch/ MktDataFull/Instrmt@Fctr =[decimal (10
)]

Message Container Open  <?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF -8"?> 
<!--Example showing only Futures --> 
<FIXML  xmlns ="http://www.fixprotocol.org/FIXML -5-0-SP2" xmlns:xsi ="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema -instance "

  <MktDataFull  RptID ="1" BizDt ="2012 -07-23" MDFeedTyp ="PR" MktID ="XKBT"> 
   <!-- Contract  Information --> 
   <Instrmt  Sym="KW" ID="KW" Src="H" SecTyp ="FUT" MMY ="201209 " MatDt ="2012 -09-14" Exch ="XKBT" Desc ="Hard Red Winter Wheat 
Futures "> 
    <Evnt EventTyp ="23" Dt="2012 -09-14"/> 
   </Instrmt > 
   <!-- Total Trading Volume --> 
   <Full Typ="B" TrdTyp ="0" TrdVol ="11071.00 00000000"/> 
   <!-- EP Trading Volume --> 
   <Full Typ="B" TrdTyp ="2" TrdVol ="805.00 00000000"/> 
   <!-- ERTrading Volume --> 
   <Full Typ="B" TrdTyp ="11" TrdVol ="0.0000000000 "/> 
   <!-- ES Trading Volume --> 
   <Full Typ="B" TrdTyp ="12" TrdVol ="0.0000000000 "/> 
   <!-- Open Interest --> 
   <Full Typ="C" TrdVol ="81048.00 00000000"/> 
   <!-- DN Stopped Volume --> 
   <Full Typ="B" TrdTyp ="3" TrdVol ="0.0000000000 "/> 
   <!-- Block Trading Volume --> 
   <Full Typ="B" TrdTyp ="1" TrdVol ="0.0000000000 "/> 
   <!-- Session Low Price --> 
   <Full Typ="2" ID="L" LowPx ="913.50 00000000" Ccy="USD " Txt="O"/> 
   <!-- Session High Price -->

 Use 
FUT|OPT  Rule Description  Error Message  Error  Type : Processing Status  
1.  F O Is Exchange provided by the Required Exchange Fields are missing.  External: Bad Record is not processed i.e. not moved to ISS 
database but is moved to Error table for external notification and

Reporter?  Data Managers view.  
2.  F O Is Valid Exchange provided?  Either Invalid Exchange code or Exchange 
Code has not  been set up in CFTC System  Internal (Record Not Processed):  Bad Record is not processed, i.e., 
not moved to ISS database. Once the data has been fixed in the 
CFTC System, the Data Manager will trigger the processing of these 
records from Error table and push it to ISS Database.  
3.  F O Is commodity provided by the 
Reporter?  Required Commodity Fields are missing.  External: Bad Record is not processed i.e. not moved to ISS 
database but is moved to Error table for external notification and 
Data Managers view.  
4.  F O Is Valid Commodity provided?  Either Invalid Commodity code or 
Commodity Code has not  been set up in 
CFTC System  Internal (Record Not Processed):  Bad Record is not processed, i.e., 
not moved to ISS database. Once the data has been fixed in the 
CFTC System, the Data Manager will trigger the processing of these 
records from Error table and push it to ISS Database.  
5.  F O If options -only contract, it cannot be 
reported as a future.  Options -only contract cannot be reported 
as a future.  Internal (Record Not Processed):  Bad Record is not processed, i.e., 
not moved to ISS database. Once the data has been fixed in the 
CFTC S ystem, the Data Manager will trigger the processing of these 
records from Error table and push it to ISS Database.  
6.  F O Is contract market active?  Contract market should be active.  Internal (Record Not Processed):  Bad Record is not processed, i.e., 
not moved to ISS database. Once the data has been fixed in the 
CFTC System, the Data Manager will trigger the processing of these 
records from Error table and push it to ISS Database.  
7.  F O Is the futures expiration dat e  a valid 
month for the contract?  Expiration Date does not contain valid 
Month.  Internal of what type?  
8.  F O Is report date > last processing 
date?  Report Date should not be greater than 
the Last Processing Date.  Internal (Record Processed):  These are for informational purposes 
only. The record will be processed i.e. record will be moved to ISS 
database and internal users will be notified about it.

Price  should be Numeric  External:  Bad Record is not processed i.e. not moved to ISS 
database but is moved to Errored table for external notification and 
Data Managers view.

Appendix B:  SFTP Account Registration  
To register an SFTP account:  
1. Browse  to the Account Creation Page on the Commission’s website, 
https://services.cftc.gov/CreateCFTCAccount/CreateLoginAccount.aspx . 
2. Confirm that you  have read the agreement and  agree to abide by its terms by selecting  the 
Agreement to Terms of Use check  box and click ing Agree . 
Commodity Futures Trading Commission  
Office of Data and Technology  Guidebook for Part 16  
 
January 02, 2014   Page 64 of 560 
 
 
3. On the Request Account Creation  page , supply the following information : 
 Requester first n ame  – The first name of the user requesting the account  
 Requester last n ame  – The last name (or surname) of the user requesting the account  
 Company n ame  – The Company that will be supplying the data to the CFTC  

Commodity Futures Trading Commission  
Office of Data and Technology  Guidebook for Part 16  
 
January 02, 2014   Page 65 of 560 
 
 Email a ddress  – The email address of the contact.  The email address must be from the 
domain that wil l be submitting data; the Reporting Entities domain.  Third party email 
domains (e.g., hotmail, yahoo, gmail) will not be accepted.  
 Telephone  – The requeste r’s phone number, should  CFTC need to confirm the user via a 
phone call.  
 Fax – Not required  
 
Once you have  submitted the data, the request will be passed to CFTC’s Office of Data and Technology 
for approval.  
 
 
4. Once the account creation is approved, you will be sent an email with a link to confirm the 
request.  Note  the three -letter Alpha Code  that mus t be used for all data submissions made by 
this company to the CFTC.  

Commodity Futures Trading Commission  
Office of Data and Technology  Guidebook for Part 16  
 
January 02, 2014   Page 66 of 560 
 
 
5. Click  the confirmation link in the email (or copy the URL into your web  browser) .  
6. On the Confirm Your Request screen , confirm the account creation request by typing in the 
three -letter  Alpha Code  supplied in the email  and click Confirm . 
 
A message will display indicating that your  request has been submitted.  

Commodity Futures Trading Commission  
Office of Data and Technology  Guidebook for Part 16  
 
January 02, 2014   Page 67 of 560 
 
 
You will receive two follow -on emails from the CFTC.  Each email will address guidelines fo r 
using this account. The first  email will contain your new user  ID and instructions on converting 
your  FTP Ac count to a Secure FTP Account. All entities that are providing Part 16 reporting must 
use Secure FTP to transmit their data.  
 
 
7. All reporting entities must exchange their Public  Keys with the CFTC to acti vate their Secure FTP 
account. Send  your Public Key  to FTPSupport@cftc.gov .  
 

Commodity Futures Trading Commission  
Office of Data and Technology  Guidebook for Part 16  
 
January 02, 2014   Page 68 of 560 
 
You will then receive the second email, which will contain your  new password for the FTP account.  
 
Commodity Futures Trading Commission  
Office of Data and Technology  Guidebook for Part 16  
 
January 02, 2014    Page 69 of 560
